The app currently assumes UTC, which is at odds with the server's timezone. This is resulting in incorrect time displays in several locations. The plan is to explicitly insert UTC timestamps via `getCurrentDatetime()` in the `pp-adapter.php` and use the user's timezone when displaying in `history.php`. There's a concern about displaying past entries, because existing database entries are in the wrong timezone.\n\n\n**Revising Time Display Logic**\n\nI'm now zeroing in on discrepancies in timestamp display. It seems I miscalculated and the previous fix in `history.php` isn't entirely correct, since the displayed time in the screenshot is `13:17:00`, which implies a 3-hour difference, not the 6 I anticipated from the server's timezone being `Asia/Dhaka`. I need to handle how the time will display for past updates. I can't easily retroactively correct the historical data. The user knows it is wrong. Webhook Listener (IPN)\n56: \n57: Once the user completes the payment, or if the admin approves the payment, Profess0rPay will send a `POST` request to the `webhook_url` you provided.\n58: \n59: **Method:** `POST`\n60: **Content-Type:** `application/json`\n61: \n62: **Payload Example Received by Your Server:**\n63: ```json\n64: {\n65:   \"pp_id\": \"893748937498\",\n66:   \"status\": \"completed\",\n67:   \"amount\": 500,\n68:   \"fee\": 5,\n69:   \"total\": 495,\n70:   \"metadata\": {\n71:     \"order_id\": \"ORD-12345\"\n72:   },\n73:   \"transaction_id\": \"BKASH12345\",\n74:   \"date\": \"Oct 25, 2023 10:30 AM\"\n75: }\n76: ```\n77: \n78: ### Example Webhook Implementation (PHP)\n79: Save this code in your `webhook.php` file:\n80: \n81: ```php\n82: <?php\n83: // Receive JSON payload\n84: $rawInput = file_get_contents(\"php://input\");\n85: $data = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n86: \n87: if ($data && isset($data['status'])) {\n88:     // Check if payment is successful\n89:     if ($data['status'] === 'completed') {\n90:         $order_id = $data['metadata']['order_id'] ?? null;\n91:         $amount = $data['amount'] ?? 0;\n92:         $transaction_id = $data['transaction_id'] ?? '';\n93: \n94:         // TODO: Validate order_id and amount with your database\n95:         // TODO: Update your database (e.g., mark order as PAID)\n96:         // TODO: Deliver the product to the customer\n97: \n98:         http_response_code(200);\n99:         echo \"OK\";\n100:         exit;\n101:     }\n102: }\n103: \n104: http_response_code(400);\n105: echo \"Bad Request\";\n106: ?>\n107: ```\n108: \n109: ---\n110: \n111: ## 3. This guide provides all the necessary details to seamlessly integrate Profess0rPay's payment gateway into your website, application, or software.\n\nOur API is designed to be developer-friendly, secure, and fast. Follow the instructions below to start processing payments.\n\n---\n\n## ⚡ Quick Reference\n\n- **Base URL**: `https://yourdomain.com` *(Replace with your actual Profess0rPay domain)*\n- **Create Endpoint**: `POST /api/create-payment`\n- **Verify Endpoint**: `POST /api/verify-payment`\n- **Authentication**: `Authorization: Bearer <API_KEY>`\n- **Content-Type**: `application/json`\n\n---\n\n## 🔐 Authentication\n\nEvery request made to the Profess0rPay API must be authenticated using your unique API Key. You can pass the API Key in the headers of your HTTP request.\n\n| Header Method | Example Value | Status |\n|---|---|---|\n| **Preferred** | `Authorization: Bearer your_api_key_here` | Recommended |\n| **Alternative** | `mhs-profess0rpay-api-key: your_api_key_here` | Supported |\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]  \n> Make sure your API key has the necessary **scopes** (e.g., `Create Payment`, `Verify Payment`) enabled in your merchant dashboard, otherwise the requests will fail.\n\n---\n\n## 📝 Common Rules\n\n- Always set the header `Content-Type: application/json`.\n- The `amount` must be greater than `0`.\n- The domains you provide in `return_url` and `webhook_url` **must be whitelisted and active** in your Merchant Dashboard under the \"Domains\" section.\n- `metadata` can be used to pass custom information (like Order ID) and it will be returned intact in the webhook and verify responses.\n\n---\n\n## 1️⃣ Create Payment\n\nGenerate a hosted checkout link for your customer.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/create-payment`\n\n### Request Parameters\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `full_name` | string | **Yes** | The full name of the customer. *(Alias: `customer_name`)* |\n| `email_address` | string | **Yes** | Customer's valid email address. *(Alias: `customer_email`)* |\n| `mobile_number` | string | **Yes** | Customer's mobile number. *(Alias: `customer_mobile`)* |\n| `amount` | number | **Yes** | The exact invoice amount (must be positive). |\n| `currency` | string | No | Currency code. Default is `BDT`. |\n| `return_url` | string | **Yes** | URL to redirect the customer after payment. *(Alias: `redirect_url`, `cancel_url`)* |\n| `webhook_url` | string | No | URL where the server-to-server callback will be sent. |\n| `metadata` | object | No | Custom JSON object to track order data (e.g., `{\"order_id\": \"123\"}`). |\n\n### Response Example\n\n```json\n{\n  \"status\": true,\n  \"message\": \"Payment created successfully\",\n  \"checkout_url\": \"https://yourdomain.com/payment/PAYMENT_ID\"\n}\n```\n\n> [!TIP]\n> **Action:** Automatically redirect your customer to the `checkout_url` provided in the response.\n\n### 💻 Code Examples: Create Payment\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>PHP (cURL)</b></summary>\n\n```php\n<?php\n$payload = [\n    \"full_name\" => \"John Doe\",\n    \"email_address\" => \"john@example.com\",\n    \"mobile_number\" => \"01700000000\",\n    \"amount\" => 1200,\n    \"currency\" => \"BDT\",\n    \"return_url\" => \"https://merchant.com/success\",\n    \"webhook_url\" => \"https://merchant.com/api/webhook\",\n    \"metadata\" => [\n        \"order_id\" => \"ORD-1001\",\n        \"customer_id\" => \"CUS-9001\"\n    ]\n];\n\n$ch = curl_init(\"https://yourdomain.com/api/create-payment\");\ncurl_setopt_array($ch, [\n    CURLOPT_POST => true,\n    CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER => true,\n    CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER => [\n        \"Content-Type: application/json\",\n        \"Authorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY\",\n    ],\n    CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS => json_encode($payload),\n]);\n\n$response = curl_exec($ch);\ncurl_close($ch);\n\necho $response;\n?>\n```\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>JavaScript (Fetch)</b></summary>\n\n```javascript\nconst response = await response.json();\nconsole.log(data.checkout_url);\n```\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>Python (Requests)</b></summary>\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\nresponse = requests.post(\n \"https://merchant.com/success\",\n        \"metadata\": {\"order_id\": \"ORD-1001\"}\n    }\n)\n\nprint(response.json())\n```\n</details>\n\n---\n\n## 2️⃣ Verify Payment\n\nSecurely check the status of a specific payment transaction from your backend.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/verify-payment`\n\n### Request Parameters\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `pp_id` | string | **Yes** | The Profess0rPay Reference ID (found at the end of the `checkout_url` or from the webhook payload). |\n\n### Response Example\n\n```json\n{\n  \"pp_id\": \"REF123456789\",\n  \"full_name\": \"John Doe\",\n  \"email_address\": \"john@example.com\",\n  \"mobile_number\": \"01700000000\",\n  \"gateway\": \"bKash\",\n  \"amount\": 1200,\n  \"fee\": 10,\n  \"discount_amount\": 0,\n  \"total\": 1190,\n  \"local_net_amount\": 1190,\n  \"currency\": \"BDT\",\n  \"local_currency\": \"BDT\",\n  \"metadata\": {\n    \"order_id\": \"ORD-1001\"\n  },\n  \"sender\": \"017XXXXXXXX\",\n  \"transaction_id\": \"BKASH_TRX_999\",\n  \"status\": \"completed\",\n  \"date\": \"Jul 09, 2026 10:30 AM\"\n}\n```\n\n> [!WARNING]\n> Only deliver the service/product if the `\"status\"` is exactly `\"completed\"` and the `\"amount\"` matches your database record.\n\n---\n\n## 3️⃣ Webhook (IPN) Integration\n\nA webhook is an automatic server-to-server callback. When a customer successfully pays or a transaction is approved by the admin, Profess0rPay will send a `POST` request to your `webhook_url` instantly.\n\n### Webhook Payload\nThe webhook receives the exact same JSON payload structure as the **Verify Payment** response. \n\n### Webhook Best Practices\n1. **Always verify:** When your webhook script receives a payload, extract the `pp_id` and call the `/api/verify-payment` endpoint to securely confirm that the callback wasn't spoofed.\n2. **Respond with 200 OK:** Your script must return an HTTP status code `200` to acknowledge receipt. If Profess0rPay does not receive a `200 OK` response, it will retry sending the webhook automatically!\n\n### Example Webhook Script (PHP)\n\n```php\n<?php\n// Receive JSON payload\n$rawInput = file_get_contents(\"php://input\");\n$data = json_decode($rawInput, true);\n\nif ($data && isset($data['status'])) {\n    \n    // Check if the payment is completed\n    if ($data['status'] === 'completed') {\n        \n        $order_id = $data['metadata']['order_id'] ?? null;\n        $amount = $data['amount'];\n        $transaction_id = $data['transaction_id'];\n        \n        // TODO: Look up $order_id in your database\n        // TODO: Validate that the $amount matches the order total\n        \n        // Mark order as PAID and deliver the product!\n        \n        http_response_code(200);\n        echo \"Webhook processed successfully\";\n        exit;\n    }\n}\n\nhttp_response_code(400);\necho \"Bad Request\";\n?>\n```\n\n---\n\n## 💡 Recommended Merchant Flow\n\n1. **Create Order:** User initiates checkout on your website. Save the order as `PENDING` in your database.\n2. **Create Invoice:** Call `POST /api/create-payment` with the user's details and your Order ID in the `metadata`.\n3. **Redirect:** Send the user to the received `checkout_url`.\n4. **Receive Webhook:** Profess0rPay sends a callback to your `webhook_url` when the user pays.\n5. **Update Database:** In your webhook script, verify the status, update your order to `PAID`, and fulfill the service.\n6. **Thank You Page:** The user is redirected back to your `return_url` to see a success message. (Do not run sensitive database updates on this page, rely on the webhook).\n\nHappy Coding! 🚀","Description":"Write the precise and beautiful API documentation to docs/API_DOCUMENTATION.md.","Overwrite":true,"TargetFile":"c:\\xampp\\htdocs\\Profess0rPay\\docs\\API_DOCUMENTATION.md","toolAction":"Write API Documentation","toolSummary":"Update API_DOCUMENTATION.md"}}]}

{"step_index":345,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-07-09T11:26:11Z","content":"প্লাগিন (Plugin) বা মডিউল (Module) হলো রেডিমেড কোডের একটি ছোট প্যাকেজ। এর মূল উদ্দেশ্য হলো— যারা কোডিং জানে না, তারা যেন জাস্ট কয়েক ক্লিকেই তাদের ওয়েবসাইটে আপনার **Profess0rPay** গেটওয়ে বসিয়ে ফেলতে পারে।\n\nআপনার প্রশ্নগুলোর উত্তর আমি একদম সহজ ভাষায় ধাপে ধাপে বুঝিয়ে দিচ্ছি:\n\n### ১. প্লাগিন কীভাবে তৈরি হয়? (How they are made)\nপ্লাগিন তৈরি করেন সফটওয়্যার ডেভেলপাররা। এই যে আমি মাত্র আপনার `API_DOCUMENTATION.md` বানালাম, একজন ডেভেলপার সেই ডকুমেন্টেশন পড়বে। এরপর সে নির্দিষ্ট কোনো প্ল্যাটফর্মের (যেমন- WordPress বা WHMCS) জন্য কিছু PHP কোড লিখবে, যেখানে আপনার `create-payment` এবং `verify-payment` API-গুলো অটোমেটিক কল হওয়ার লজিক দেওয়া থাকবে। কোড লেখা শেষে ফাইলগুলোকে জিপ (Zip) করে একটি প্লাগিন বানানো হয়।\n\n### ২. প্লাগিন কোথায় অ্যাড করে? (Where are they added)\nপ্লাগিন কখনোই আপনার (Profess0rPay-এর) মেইন সার্ভারে অ্যাড করতে হয় না। \nপ্লাগিন অ্যাড করতে হয় **মার্চেন্টের (যে আপনার গেটওয়ে ব্যবহার করবে) ওয়েবসাইটে**। \nধরুন, একজনের একটি WordPress ই-কমার্স সাইট আছে। সে আপনার \"Profess0rPay WooCommerce Plugin\" জিপ ফাইলটি ডাউনলোড করবে। এরপর তার ওয়ার্ডপ্রেসের অ্যাডমিন প্যানেলে গিয়ে `Plugins > Add New`-তে ক্লিক করে জিপ ফাইলটি আপলোড করে দিবে। ব্যাস, আপনার পেমেন্ট গেটওয়ে তার সাইটে যুক্ত হয়ে যাবে!\n\n### ৩. কীভাবে কাজ করে? (How it works)\nপ্লাগিন ব্যাকএন্ডে আপনার API-এর সাথেই কথা বলে। পুরো প্রসেসটা এরকম:\n- কাস্টমার মার্চেন্টের সাইটে গিয়ে কোনো প্রোডাক্ট কিনে \"Pay with Profess0rPay\" বাটনে ক্লিক করবে।\n- প্লাগিনটি তখন অটোমেটিক মার্চেন্টের সাইট থেকে অর্ডার অ্যামাউন্ট ও কাস্টমারের ডিটেইলস নিয়ে আপনার `api/create-payment` API-তে রিকোয়েস্ট পাঠাবে।\n- আপনার API একটি `checkout_url` দিবে, প্লাগিনটি তখন কাস্টমারকে সেই লিংকে রিডাইরেক্ট করে দিবে।\n- কাস্টমার পেমেন্ট করলে আপনার সিস্টেম থেকে মার্চেন্টের সাইটে Webhook যাবে।\n- প্লাগিনটি সেই Webhook রিসিভ করে অটোমেটিক কাস্টমারের অর্ডারটি \"Paid\" করে দিবে।\n\n### ৪. প্লাগিনের সুবিধা কী? (Benefits)\n- **কোডিং নলেজ ছাড়াই ইন্টিগ্রেশন:** মার্চেন্ট বা ওয়েবসাইটের মালিকদের কোনো ডেভেলপার হায়ার করতে হয় না। জাস্ট প্লাগিন ইন্সটল করবে এবং আপনার দেওয়া **API Key** বসিয়ে দিবে। ৫ মিনিটেই গেটওয়ে রেডি!\n- **মার্কেট বৃদ্ধি (Huge User Base):** ZiniPay-এর মতো আপনার যদি রেডিমেড WordPress, WHMCS বা Laravel প্লাগিন থাকে, তাহলে হাজার হাজার মানুষ খুব সহজেই আপনার গেটওয়ে ইউজ করতে চাইবে। কারণ তাদের কোনো প্যারা নিতে হচ্ছে না। \n- **ভুল বা এরর কম হয়:** মার্চেন্টরা নিজে নিজে কোড করে API বসাতে গেলে অনেক বাগ বা সিকিউরিটি ইস্যু হতে পারে। আপনার অফিশিয়াল প্লাগিন থাকলে সবাই ১০০% সিকিউর ও স্মুথ এক্সপেরিয়েন্স পাবে।\n\n**সংক্ষেপে বলতে গেলে:** আপনার API ডকুমেন্টেশন হলো ইঞ্জিনের ম্যানুয়াল, আর প্লাগিন হলো রেডিমেড গাড়ি। কাস্টমার শুধু চাবি (API Key) ঘুরাবে আর গাড়ি চলবে! \n\nআপনি চাইলে আমরা ধীরে ধীরে পপুলার প্ল্যাটফর্মগুলোর (যেমন- WooCommerce/WordPress) জন্য Profess0rPay-এর অফিশিয়াল প্লাগিন তৈরি করা শুরু করতে পারি।","thinking":"**Prioritizing Tool Usage**\n\nI'm now focusing on tool selection, emphasizing specific tools over general ones where possible. অনেক গোছানো। তবে এর জন্য কিছুটা সময় এবং টেকনিক্যাল নলেজ দরকার হয়। \n\nপ্লাগিন তৈরি করার সময় এবং চ্যালেঞ্জগুলো নিচে বিস্তারিত তুলে ধরলাম:\n\n### ⏳ প্লাগিন বানাতে কেমন সময় লাগে?\nপ্লাগিন বানানোর সময় বানাতে **১ থেকে ২ দিন** সময় লাগতে পারে। \n২. **WHMCS / SMM Panels / PerfexCRM:** এগুলোর নিজস্ব কিছু আলাদা স্ট্রাকচার আছে। প্রতিটি মডিউল বানাতে এবং টেস্ট করতে গড়ে **১ থেকে ৩ দিন** সময় লাগতে পারে।\n৩. **Laravel SDK / PHP Library:** আপনার API দিয়ে একটি সুন্দর প্যাকেজ বা লাইব্রেরি বানাতে **কয়েক ঘণ্টা থেকে ১ দিন** লাগতে পারে।\n\n*অর্থাৎ, আপনি যদি প্রথম ধাপে সবচেয়ে জনপ্রিয় ৫-৬টি প্ল্যাটফর্মের (যেমন- WordPress, WHMCS, SMM Panel) জন্য প্লাগিন বানাতে চান, তবে টানা কাজ করলে ১-২ সপ্তাহের মধ্যে সবগুলো রেডি করে ফেলা সম্ভব। (আর আমাকে ইনস্ট্রাকশন দিলে আমি হয়তো কয়েক ঘণ্টার মধ্যেই একেকটি প্লাগিনের ফুল কোড রেডি করে দিতে পারবো!)*\n\n---\n\n### 🧗 কী কী চ্যালেঞ্জ বা Difficulty আছে?\nপ্লাগিন বানাতে গেলে ডেভেলপারদের সাধারণত নিচের বিষয়গুলো খেয়াল রাখতে হয়:\n\n১. **আলাদা আলাদা আর্কিটেকচার (Different Ecosystems):** \nWordPress-এ যেভাবে কোড কাজ করে, WHMCS বা Shopify-তে সেভাবে কাজ করে না। প্রতিটি প্ল্যাটফর্মের নিজস্ব নির্দিষ্ট নিয়ম (Documentation) আছে। ডেভেলপারকে আগে সেই প্ল্যাটফর্মের নিয়ম পড়তে হয়, তারপর সে অনুযায়ী আপনার API বসাতে হয়।\n\n২. **সিকিউরিটি ও ফেক পেমেন্ট ঠেকানো:**\nসবচেয়ে বড় চ্যালেঞ্জ হলো Webhook বা IPN হ্যান্ডেল করা। প্লাগিনের ভেতরে এমন কোড লিখতে হয় যেন কোনো হ্যাকার ভুয়া (Fake) Webhook রিকোয়েস্ট পাঠিয়ে ফ্রিতে প্রোডাক্ট কিনে নিতে না পারে। এজন্য প্লাগিনকে অর্ডার স্ট্যাটাস আপডেট করার আগে অবশ্যই আপনার `verify-payment` API কল করে ডাবল চেক করে নিতে হয়। \n\n৩. **ভার্সন আপডেট ও মেইনটেন্যান্স (Compatibility):**\nWordPress বা অন্যান্য প্ল্যাটফর্মগুলো নিয়মিত আপডেট হয়। দেখা গেলো, আজকে আপনি প্লাগিন বানালেন, ২ বছর পর WooCommerce-এর নতুন আপডেটে সেই কোড সাপোর্ট করছে না। তখন IS LIVE!**  \n> OmniPay now fully supports **Dhru Fusion** billing panels natively! You can now auto-verify Mobile Financial Services (MFS) and Crypto deposits on IMEI, telecom, and file unlocking portals. Download the official gateway module directly from the developer dashboard downloads page.\n\n<p align=\"center\">\n  <a href=\"#-the-omnipay-vision\">The Vision</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-core-features--gateways\">Features</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-system-architecture\">Architecture</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-core-components-breakdown\">Codebase Breakdown</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-installation--deployment\">Installation</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-comprehensive-api-reference\">API Docs</a> •\n  <a href=\"#-plugin-development\">Development</a>\n</p>\n\n---\n\n## 🌍 The OmniPay Vision (Why It's a Game Changer)\n\nTraditional payment gateways lock merchants into rigid ecosystems. They charge exorbitant transaction fees (2% to 5%), dictate terms of service that can result in frozen funds, and limit operations based on geography. \n\n**OmniPay is not a traditional payment processor. It is a self-hosted orchestration engine.**\n\nOmniPay connects your existing personal accounts (bKash, Nagad, Binance, Metamask) and bridges them into an automated checkout pipeline. By reading confirmation SMS messages from your phone and tracking on-chain blockchain data, OmniPay auto-verifies transactions. \n\n### The OmniPay Advantage:\n* **World-First iOS Support:** The ONLY aggregator platform allowing seamless, background SMS payment forwarding from an iPhone (no jailbreak required).\n* **Dhru Fusion Integration:** Built-in billing and automation module for telecom, IMEI, and file unlocking portals running on Dhru Fusion.\n* **Zero Platform Fees:** Since the payment flows directly to your personal wallets or MFS accounts, there is no intermediary charging a percentage.\n* **No Vendor Lock-in:** You deploy the OmniPay server on your own infrastructure (VPS or shared hosting). Your data, invoices, and customer details remain yours.\n* **Unified Checkout:** Provide your customers a beautiful, single-page experience that supports local mobile banking and global cryptocurrencies simultaneously.\n* **Extensible & Open-Source:** Need a new local payment method? Write a simple PHP class implementing the `PaymentDriverInterface`. \n* **Multi-Tenant System:** Built for scale. A single OmniPay installation can power multiple \"Stores,\" allowing you to act as a payment provider for your other businesses or clients.\n\n---\n\n## ✨ Core Features & Gateways\n\n### 💳 Supported Payment Gateways\n\nOmniPay ships with **10 Production-Ready Drivers** out of the box.\n\n| Gateway / Network | Type | Verification Mechanism | Status |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| **bKash** | Mobile Financial Service | Tokenized API & Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **Nagad** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **Rocket** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **Upay** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **CellFin (IBBL)** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **OK Wallet** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **Tap** | Mobile Financial Service | Personal (SMS Sync) | ✅ Ready |\n| **Binance Pay** | Crypto Exchange | Binance REST API Verification | ✅ Ready |\n| **Bybit Pay** | Crypto Exchange | Bybit REST API Verification | ✅ Ready |\n| **Web3 (BSC, ETH, TRON, OP, ARB)** | Decentralized Blockchain | Block Explorer API (Etherscan, TronGrid, BscScan) | ✅ Ready |\n\n### 🔌 Supported Client Integrations & Modules\nWe support native plugin integrations for the following popular billing, hosting, and SMM panel portals:\n* **WHMCS**: Process client checkouts and automate payment tracking inside WHMCS.\n* **Dhru Fusion**: Auto-verify deposits and credit user balances on IMEI, file unlocking, and telecom portals.\n* **Blesta**: Accept payments and manage client credit billing natively.\n* **WooCommerce**: Unified, branded payment checkouts for WordPress storefronts.\n* **SMM Panels**: Automatically top up user balances on popular SMM script services.\n\n### 🛠️ Platform Capabilities\n\n* **Intelligent Auto-Verification System:** Employs a unique \"fractional offset\" algorithm. If an invoice is for $25.00, OmniPay asks for $25.000384 to perfectly match incoming SMS or crypto transactions to the exact invoice, solving the concurrency problem of multiple users paying the same amount at the same time.\n* **Multi-Store Architecture:** Merchants can create isolated stores. Each store has its own independent API key, Webhook callback URLs, and payment gateway configurations.\n* **Intelligent MFS Parser:** The built-in `MfsParser` service can understand complex SMS structures from 8 different mobile banking providers, extracting TrxIDs, sender numbers, and amounts automatically.\n* **Web Installer Wizard:** Zero-CLI setup. Just upload the files, navigate to `/install`, and the wizard handles database connections, migrations, and admin user creation.\n* **HMAC-SHA256 Webhooks:** Secure server-to-server callbacks ensure that your frontend/billing system (like WHMCS, Dhru Fusion) only processes legitimate payment confirmations.\n* **Sandbox Mode:** Test transactions locally without real money.\n\n## 📸 Screenshots & Platform Overview\n\n### Core Gateways Management\nEnable and disable multiple payment gateways globally, such as bKash, Binance, and Web3 wallets, and easily upload custom gateway logos.\n![Core Gateways](<Screenshots/1 (1).png>)\n\n### Dashboard Overview\nView high-level metrics like processed volume, success rate, average ticket size, and revenue charts. Connect your Android SMS Sync App directly via the provided QR code.\n![Dashboard Top](<Screenshots/1 (2).png>)\n![Dashboard Bottom](<Screenshots/1 (3).png>)\n\n### Storefront Management\nManage multiple merchant stores, view active profiles, and register new API-isolated storefronts with ease.\n![My Stores](<Screenshots/1 (4).png>)\n\n### Invoice Generation\nCreate custom invoices and direct payment links straight from the admin panel.\n![Create Invoice](<Screenshots/1 (5).png>)\n\n### Invoice Logs\nTrack, filter, and manage all invoice transactions including Paid, Pending, Refunded, and Expired statuses.\n![Invoices](<Screenshots/1 (6).png>)\n\n### Customer Checkout Page\nA clean, modern payment request page providing customers with all enabled local and global payment options.\n![Checkout Page](<Screenshots/1 (7).png>)\n\n### API Request Logs\nMonitor API traffic and debug requests with detailed logs including endpoint, method, status, duration, and IP address.\n![API Logs](<Screenshots/1 (8).png>)\n\n### Security & Global Settings\nConfigure critical system controls like Multi-Merchant access, Dynamic Math Captcha, and global SMTP email settings.\n![Security Settings](<Screenshots/1 (9).png>)\n\n### Mobile App - SMS Sync Integration\nConnect and monitor the Android SMS Sync app to auto-verify mobile financial service transactions silently in the background.\n<p align=\"center\">\n  <img src=\"Screenshots/WhatsApp Image 2026-06-20 at 2.18.11 PM.jpeg\" width=\"300\" alt=\"Mobile App Login\">\n  <img src=\"Screenshots/WhatsApp Imagje 2026-06-20 at 2.18.11 PM.jpeg\" width=\"300\" alt=\"Mobile App Dashboard\">\n</p>\n\n---\n\n## 🏗️ System Architecture\n\nOmniPay is built on the robust **Laravel 12** framework.\n\n### Flow Diagram\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n    Client[Client Browser] --> |Checkout Link| OP_UI(OmniPay Checkout UI)\n    Billing[Billing System / WHMCS] -->|POST /api/v1/payment| OP_API(OmniPay REST API)\n    OP_API --> |Returns Checkout Token| Billing\n    \n    OP_UI --> |Selects Method| PluginMgr[Payment Gateway Manager]\n    PluginMgr --> bKash[bKash Driver]\n    PluginMgr --> Binance[Binance Driver]\n    PluginMgr --> Web3[Web3 Driver]\n    PluginMgr --> SMS[SMS Sync Drivers]\n    \n    SMS_App[Android SMS Sync App] --> |POST /api/v1/sync-sms| SMS_Pool(Synced Transactions Pool)\n    SMS_Pool -.-> |Matches Amount + TrxID| SMS\n    \n    Blockchain[Block Explorers API] -.-> |Polls TX Hash| Web3\n    \n    bKash --> |Status: Paid| Webhook[Webhook Dispatcher]\n    Binance --> |Status: Paid| Webhook\n    Web3 --> |Status: Paid| Webhook\n    SMS --> |Status: Paid| Webhook\n    \n    Webhook --> |HMAC Signed POST| Billing\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🧩 Core Components Breakdown\n\nOmniPay is highly modular. Understanding the core Models, Services, and Controllers will allow you to confidently modify or extend the engine.\n\n### 🗄️ Models (The Data Layer)\n\n| Model | Description & Responsibilities |\n|---|---|\n| **`User`** | Represents the platform users. Users can be `admin` (global control) or `merchant` (manages their own stores). Contains attributes for Two-Factor Authentication (`two_factor_secret`), notification preferences, and the critical `sms_sync_key` used by the Android App to map incoming SMS data to a specific merchant. |\n| **`Store`** | Represents a merchant's business entity. A `User` can have many `Stores`. Each store generates a unique `api_key` which is used by external billing systems (WHMCS, WooCommerce) to create invoices on behalf of this store. |\n| **`PaymentMethod`** | A global dictionary of available payment gateways (e.g., code `bkash`, `binance`, `web3`). |\n| **`StorePaymentConfig`** | The pivot model between a `Store` and a `PaymentMethod`. It stores the merchant's specific credentials (e.g., API keys, Wallet Addresses, Personal Phone Numbers) in a JSON `settings` column. |\n| **`Invoice`** | The central ledger. Records `amount` (base cost), `expected_amount` (cost + micro-offset for tracing), `status` (pending/paid/expired), and the generated `payment_link`. Uses Eloquent Events to automatically fire Webhooks and send Email Notifications when the status changes to `paid`. |\n| **`SyncedTransaction`** | A temporary holding pool. When the Android SMS App reads a payment text message, it pushes the data here via the API. Payment Drivers constantly query this table to find matches for pending Invoices. Once a match is found and applied to an invoice, the record is destroyed to prevent double-spending. |\n\n### ⚙️ Services (The Logic Layer)\n\n| Service | Description & Responsibilities |\n|---|---|\n| **`PaymentGatewayManager`** | A registry for the plugin system. On boot, all available Payment Drivers (implementing `PaymentDriverInterface`) are registered here. Controllers use this manager to resolve the correct driver dynamically based on the user's selection at checkout. |\n| **`MfsParser`** | The brain behind the SMS parsing. Contains complex regex rules mapped by priority for various Mobile Financial Services (bKash, Nagad, Rocket, Upay, CellFin). Extracts `amount`, `trxid`, and `sender` from raw, unstructured text messages. It handles English/Bengali variations and gracefully falls back to generic extraction if strict regexes fail. |\n| **`MailNotificationService`** | Handles all outbound SMTP emails using Laravel's Mail facade. Sends beautiful HTML receipts for `InvoiceCreated`, `InvoicePaid`, and `InvoiceExpired` events to the customer, and alerts the merchant if a manual intervention is required. |\n| **`TotpService`** | Implements Time-Based One-Time Passwords (RFC 6238) for merchant and admin dashboard security (Google Authenticator compatibility). |\n| **`CaptchaService`** | Verifies hCaptcha tokens to protect login, registration, and password reset endpoints from bot abuse. |\n\n### 🎛️ Controllers (The Routing Layer)\n\n| Controller | Description & Responsibilities |\n|---|---|\n| **`Api\\InvoiceController`** | Provides the `POST /api/v1/payment` endpoint. Validates the Store API Key, generates the unique micro-fractional `expected_amount` offset, creates the `Invoice`, and generates the base64-encoded checkout URL token. |\n| **`Api\\SmsSyncController`** | Provides the `POST /api/v1/sync-sms` endpoint for the Android App. Validates the `sms_sync_key`, calls the `MfsParser` service to decode the SMS, and creates a `SyncedTransaction` record. Prevents replay attacks by ensuring duplicate TrxIDs are rejected. |\n| **`CheckoutController`** | Powers the public-facing checkout UI. Handles token decoding (`show`), payment method selection (`selectMethod`), continuous AJAX polling for payment verification (`checkStatus`), and sandbox mode simulations. It dynamically calls the `initiatePayment` and `verifyPayment` methods on the selected Gateway Driver. |\n| **`DashboardController`** | The massive backend controller managing the Merchant and Admin portals. Handles CRUD operations for Stores, updating Payment Gateway configurations, viewing/refunding/deleting Invoices, managing QR codes, and viewing API/Activity logs. |\n| **`InstallController`** | Powers the web-based setup wizard. Validates PHP extensions, tests MySQL connections, creates the database schema dynamically if missing, runs Laravel migrations/seeds, and writes the `storage/installed` lock file to prevent re-execution. |\n| **`Api\\AppTransactionController`** | Used by the frontend Merchant Dashboard and mobile merchant apps to list, view, and manually manage (mark paid/cancelled) invoices and synced transactions via REST API. |\n| **`Api\\GatewayCompatibilityController`** | Provides legacy endpoints (`/api/create-charge`, `/api/verify-payments`) to ensure OmniPay remains backwards compatible with older PipraPay modules used in legacy WHMCS setups. |\n\n---\n\n## 📁 Directory Structure\n\n```text\nomnipay/\n├── app/\n│   ├── Contracts/              # Interfaces (PaymentDriverInterface)\n│   ├── Http/\n│   │   ├── Controllers/        # Core Application Logic\n│   │   │   ├── Api/            # REST API endpoints (Invoice, Sync, Compat)\n│   │   │   ├── AuthController  # Login, Register, 2FA\n│   │   │   ├── CheckoutController # Public Payment Flow\n│   │   │   └── DashboardController # Admin & Merchant Panel\n│   │   └── Middleware/         # Request Interceptors (Auth, API Logs, Install Check)\n│   ├── Models/                 # Eloquent ORM Models\n│   ├── Plugins/                # 💳 Payment Gateway Drivers (bKash, Binance, Web3, etc.)\n│   └── Services/               # Shared Logic (MfsParser, Mailer, Totp)\n├── config/                     # Application Configuration\n├── database/\n│   ├── migrations/             # Database Schema Definitions\n│   └── seeders/                # Default Data (Gateways, Admin User)\n├── public/\n│   └── downloads/              # 🔌 Client Integrations (WHMCS, WooCommerce Zips)\n├── resources/\n│   └── views/                  # Blade Templates\n│       ├── auth/               # Authentication Screens\n│       ├── checkout/           # Public Payment Gateway UI\n│       ├── dashboard/          # Merchant & Admin Panel UI\n│       └── install/            # Setup Wizard UI\n├── routes/\n│   ├── api.php                 # API Route Definitions\n│   └── web.php                 # Web & Dashboard Route Definitions\n└── storage/                    # Logs, Cache, and 'installed' Lock file\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 Installation & Deployment\n\n### Server Requirements\n\n* **PHP:** 8.2 or higher\n* **Database:** MySQL 5.7+ or MariaDB 10.3+\n* **PHP Extensions:** `openssl`, `pdo`, `mbstring`, `tokenizer`, `xml`, `ctype`, `json`, `bcmath`, `fileinfo`\n* **Composer** (If installing via CLI)\n\n### Method 1: Web Installer (cPanel / Shared Hosting)\n\nThis is the easiest method and requires no terminal access.\n\n1. **Download:** Grab the latest release archive.\n2. **Upload:** Extract the contents into your `public_html` or designated domain folder.\n3. **Environment:** Copy `.env.example` to `.env` (ensure `SESSION_DRIVER=file` and `CACHE_STORE=file` are set).\n4. **Permissions:** Ensure `storage/` and `bootstrap/cache/` directories are writable (775).\n5. **Run Setup:** Navigate to `https://your-domain.com/install` in your browser.\n6. The setup wizard will verify requirements, ask for your MySQL credentials, create the database tables, and help you set up the Admin account.\n\n### Method 2: Command Line (VPS / Docker / Local Dev)\n\n```bash\n# 1. Clone the repository\ngit clone https://github.com/your-org/omnipay.git\ncd omnipay\n\n# 2. Install dependencies\ncomposer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev\n\n# 3. Setup environment\ncp .env.example .env\nphp artisan key:generate\n\n# 4. Edit .env with your database credentials\nnano .env \n\n# 5. Run migrations and default seeds\nphp artisan migrate --force\nphp artisan db:seed --force\n\n# 6. Optimize for production\nphp artisan optimize\n\n# 7. Start queue worker (Required for Webhook dispatching and Emails)\nphp artisan queue:work --daemon\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📡 Comprehensive API Reference\n\nOmniPay operates API-first. You can integrate any custom system by utilizing the `/api/v1/` endpoints.\n\n### Authentication\n\nAll API endpoints expect the store's unique API Key passed in the header.\n\n```http\nX-API-KEY: your_store_api_key_here\nContent-Type: application/json\nAccept: application/json\n```\n\n---\n\n### 1. Create a Payment Invoice\n\nCreates a new checkout session.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/v1/payment`\n\n**Request Payload:**\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `amount` | `float` | ✅ Yes | The payment amount (e.g., 50.00). Must be > 0. |\n| `customer_name` | `string` | ✅ Yes | The full name of the payer. |\n| `customer_email` | `string` | ✅ Yes | The email of the payer (receives receipts). |\n| `currency` | `string` | No | Base currency (Default: `USDT`). |\n| `callback_url` | `string` | No | Webhook URL for server-to-server notifications. |\n| `cancel_url` | `string` | No | Browser redirect URL if user cancels or completes. |\n| `meta_data` | `object` | No | Any custom JSON data (e.g., `{\"order_id\": 123}`). |\n| `is_sandbox` | `boolean`| No | If true, creates a simulated invoice for testing. |\n\n**Response (`201 Created`):**\n```json\n{\n  \"success\": true,\n  \"invoice_id\": \"INV-X9K2M3ZPLQ\",\n  \"amount\": 50.00,\n  \"expected_amount\": 50.000412,\n  \"currency\": \"USDT\",\n  \"payment_link\": \"https://your-domain.com/checkout/BASE64_TOKEN_HERE\",\n  \"expires_at\": \"2026-06-20 14:30:00\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Verify Payment Status\n\nCheck the current status of an invoice.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/v1/transactions/{invoice_id}`\n\n**Response (`200 OK`):**\n```json\n{\n  \"success\": true,\n  \"invoice\": {\n    \"invoice_id\": \"INV-X9K2M3ZPLQ\",\n    \"status\": \"paid\",\n    \"amount\": 50.00,\n    \"paid_at\": \"2026-06-20 14:15:00\",\n    \"meta_data\": {\n      \"order_id\": 123,\n      \"txHash\": \"0xabc123...\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. Sync SMS Notification (Mobile App Integration)\n\nThis endpoint is utilized by the companion Android Application to push incoming MFS SMS messages to the server pool.\n\n**📱 Android App Download & Setup:**\n- **Pre-built APK:** Download the ready-to-use app: [omnipay.apk](omnipay.apk)\n- **Source Code:** Download the Android Studio project: [Omnipay_androidstudio_source_code.zip](Omnipay_androidstudio_source_code.zip)\n\n**Setup Instructions:**\n1. Install `omnipay.apk` on an Android phone that receives your MFS (bKash/Nagad) SMS notifications.\n2. Open the app and grant \"SMS Read\" permissions.\n3. Log in using your OmniPay Merchant email and password, or use your `SMS Sync Key` from the dashboard.\n4. The app will run in the background. Whenever a payment SMS arrives, it immediately forwards it to your OmniPay server.\n\n### 🍎 iOS / iPhone Support via Apple Shortcuts (World First!)\n\n> **🏆 Industry First:** Other payment gateway aggregators and licensors *do not* support iPhone SMS reading. OmniPay is proud to be the **FIRST** platform in the world to implement a seamless iOS integration using Apple's native Shortcuts app! **No jailbreak required.**\n\n#### 📋 Prerequisites\n* An iPhone running **iOS 14** or later (iOS 17+ recommended for completely silent operation).\n* The native Apple **Shortcuts** app installed.\n* Your OmniPay `SMS Sync Key` (found in your Dashboard -> Settings -> Security).\n\n#### 🛠️ Step-by-Step Setup Guide\n\n**Step 1: Tell your iPhone to listen for Payment SMS**\n1. Open the **Shortcuts** app on your iPhone.\n2. Tap the **Automation** tab at the bottom.\n3. Tap the **+** (plus) icon at the top right to create a new automation.\n4. Scroll down and choose **Message**.\n5. In the \"Message Contains\" box, type your mobile banking name (like `bKash` or `Nagad`).\n6. Choose **Run Immediately** so it works automatically in the background.\n7. Tap **Next**, then choose **New Blank Automation**.\n\n**Step 2: Tell your iPhone where to send the SMS**\n1. Tap **Add Action**, search for the word `URL`, and select it.\n2. Type in your website's sync link: `https://your-domain.com/api/v1/sync-sms`\n3. Tap the search bar at the bottom again, search for `Get Contents of URL`, and add it.\n\n**Step 3: Add your Secret Key and Details**\n1. Tap the little arrow `>` next to \"Get Contents of URL\" to open its settings.\n2. Change the **Method** from `GET` to `POST`.\n3. Under **Headers**, add a new header:\n   - On the left side (Key), type: `X-API-KEY`\n   - On the right side (Text), paste your `SMS Sync Key` (Get this from your OmniPay Dashboard).\n4. Under **Request Body**, make sure it says **JSON**, then add two text fields:\n   - First field Key: `sender` | Text: `bKash` (or whatever your service is)\n   - Second field Key: `msg_data` | Text: Tap this box, and choose **Shortcut Input** from the keyboard menu.\n\n**Step 4: Get a Beautiful Native Notification (Optional but recommended!)**\n*Want your iPhone to pop up a success banner when a payment is synced?*\n1. Search for **Get Dictionary from Input** and add it. Set it to accept the **Contents of URL** response.\n2. Search for **Get Value from Dictionary** and add it. Set the key to `message`.\n3. Search for **Show Notification** and add it. Tap the text box and choose the Dictionary Value output. \n\n**Step 5: Save your Shortcut!**\n1. Tap **Done** in the top right corner.\n2. **Important:** If you are on iOS 17 or newer, make sure \"Notify When Run\" is turned **OFF**.\n\n🎉 *That's it! Your iPhone will now silently forward payment messages to your server and pop up a beautiful banner to let you know!*\n\n**Endpoint details (for custom app developers):**\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/v1/sync-sms`\n\n**Request Payload:**\n```json\n{\n  \"sender\": \"bKash\",\n  \"msg_data\": \"You have received Tk 500.00 from 017XXXXXX. TrxID X8M9KL2 at 14:10.\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Handling Webhooks (Callbacks)\n\nWhen an invoice transitions to the `paid` status, OmniPay fires a POST request to your `callback_url`.\n\nTo prevent spoofing, **you must verify the HMAC signature**. OmniPay signs the entire JSON payload using your Store API Key.\n\n**PHP Webhook Receiver Example:**\n\n```php\n<?php\n\n$payload = file_get_contents('php://input');\n$signatureHeader = $_SERVER['HTTP_X_OMNIPAY_SIGNATURE'] ?? '';\n\n$myStoreApiKey = 'your_store_api_key_here';\n$expectedSignature = hash_hmac('sha256', $payload, $myStoreApiKey);\n\nif (!hash_equals($expectedSignature, $signatureHeader)) {\n    http_response_code(403);\n    die('Invalid signature');\n}\n\n$data = json_decode($payload, true);\n\nif ($data['status'] === 'paid') {\n    $orderId = $data['meta_data']['order_id'];\n    $paidAmount = $data['amount'];\n    \n    // Process order fulfillment in your database here...\n    \n    http_response_code(200);\n    echo \"Webhook Processed\";\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🔒 Security & Best Practices\n\nRunning a payment aggregator requires strict security measures. OmniPay includes several built-in protections:\n\n### 1. Replay Attack Protection\nEvery payment driver (MFS, Binance, Web3) stores the verified `Transaction ID` (or `TxHash`) inside the invoice's `meta_data` upon successful payment. Before marking an invoice as paid, the system checks if this exact ID has already been used across any other invoice in the database.\n\n### 2. Micro-Offset Matching\nBecause personal MFS accounts do not have dynamic checkout APIs, multiple users sending `500 BDT` at the same time causes a collision. OmniPay solves this by asking User A for `500.000312 BDT` and User B for `500.000951 BDT`. When the SMS app syncs the transaction, OmniPay matches the exact decimal footprint to the correct invoice.\n\n### 3. API Key Isolation\nA Store API Key can only create and read invoices attached to that specific store. If a merchant's store key is compromised, it cannot access data from other stores on the platform. Keys can be instantly regenerated from the Dashboard.\n\n### 4. Two-Factor Authentication (2FA)\nWe strongly recommend enabling 2FA for all Admin and Merchant accounts via the **Settings -> Security** panel. This utilizes TOTP (Google Authenticator, Authy).\n\n---\n\n## 🛠️ Plugin Development (Creating Custom Gateways)\n\nAdding a new gateway, such as Stripe, PayPal, or a local bank API, takes less than 30 minutes.\n\n### 1. Create the Driver Class\n\nCreate a new file `app/Plugins/StripeDriver.php`:\n\n```php\n<?php\n\nnamespace App\\Plugins;\n\nuse App\\Contracts\\PaymentDriverInterface;\nuse App\\Models\\Invoice;\n\nclass StripeDriver implements PaymentDriverInterface\n{\n    public function getCode(): string {\n        return 'stripe'; // Unique identifier\n    }\n\n    public function getName(): string {\n        return 'Stripe Credit Card';\n    }\n\n    public function initiatePayment(Invoice $invoice, array $settings): array {\n        // Return data that will be passed to the frontend Vue/Blade checkout view\n        return [\n            'public_key' => $settings['public_key'],\n            'amount' => $invoice->amount,\n            'instructions' => 'Please enter your card details below.'\n        ];\n    }\n\n    public function verifyPayment(Invoice $invoice, array $settings, array $requestData): array {\n        // Validation logic using Stripe SDK\n        // ...\n        \n        if ($paymentSuccessful) {\n            $invoice->update(['status' => 'paid', 'paid_at' => now()]);\n            return [\n                'status' => 'success',\n                'message' => 'Card charged successfully!'\n            ];\n        }\n        \n        return ['status' => 'error', 'message' => 'Card declined.'];\n    }\n\n    public function refund(Invoice $invoice, array $settings, array $refundData): array {\n        return ['status' => 'manual', 'message' => 'Please refund via Stripe Dashboard'];\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Register the Plugin\n\n1. Register your class inside `app/Providers/AppServiceProvider.php` (or a dedicated Gateway provider) so it binds to the `PaymentGatewayManager`.\n2. Add an entry to the `payment_methods` database table with the code `stripe`.\n\nYour new gateway will instantly appear in the Admin Dashboard for merchants to configure!\n\n---\n\n## 🙋 Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)\n\n**Q: Webhooks are not being delivered to WHMCS. Why?**  \n**A:** OmniPay uses Laravel's event queue to send webhooks asynchronously. Ensure you are running a queue worker on your server (`php artisan queue:work`) or have configured your server's Supervisor service to keep the queue running.\n\n**Q: The SMS Android App says \"Invalid API Key\".**  \n**A:** Go to your OmniPay Dashboard -> Settings -> Security. You will find your `SMS Sync Key` there. This is different from the `Store API Key`.\n\n**Q: Does it support Auto-Conversion from USD to BDT?**  \n**A:** Yes! Every Store Payment Config allows you to set a custom \"Conversion Rate\". If you pass `USD` to the API, the checkout page will automatically display the equivalent amount in `BDT` to the customer based on your set rate. If you pass `BDT` directly, the conversion rate is ignored (1:1).\n\n**Q: Can I rebrand the frontend for my own company?**  \n**A:** Absolutely. OmniPay is MIT Licensed. You can change the logos in `public/`, modify the CSS, and sell access to merchants under your own brand name.\n\n---\n\n## 🤝 Contributing\n\nOmniPay thrives on community contributions. Whether it's adding new blockchain network support, a new local MFS parser regex, or improving the dashboard UI, PRs are deeply appreciated.\n\n1. **Fork** the repository on GitHub.\n2. **Clone** your fork locally.\n3. **Branch:** Create a new branch (`git checkout -b feature/awesome-new-gateway`).\n4. **Commit:** Ensure your code follows Laravel's PSR-12 coding standard (`./vendor/bin/pint`).\n5. **Push & Pull Request.**\n\n---\n\n## 📄 License\n\nOmniPay is open-source software licensed under the [MIT License](LICENSE).\n\nThis means you are absolutely free to rebrand, resell, modify, and distribute OmniPay in your commercial projects without restriction or attribution requirements.\n\n---\n\n## 📝 Changelog\n\n### [1.1.0] - 2026-06-22\n* **SMS Reader Sync App QR Overhaul**: Redesigned the SMS Sync App QR code card on the dashboard to be visually premium, featuring active pulse syncing states and a vertical laser scanning animation overlay.\n* **Canvas Center Logo Rendering**: Upgraded the QRious rendering logic to canvas-level `H` (30% error correction level) and dynamically injected the OmniPay favicon directly in the center of the QR code with a custom rounded white mask.\n* **Credentials Copy Actions**: Added inline clipboard copy helper elements with active success states for both Server URL and App Connection Key.\n* **Functional APK Download Link**: Copied `omnipay.apk` to public downloads and linked the dashboard download shortcut directly to the asset.\n\n### [1.0.0] - 2026-06-22\n* **Dhru Fusion Integration Module**: Added a fully compliant payment gateway integration module for Dhru Fusion unlocking portals. OmniPay আসলে কী?\nএটি Laravel 12 দিয়ে তৈরি একটি ওপেন-সোর্স পেমেন্ট সিস্টেম। এর সবচেয়ে বড় সুবিধা হলো, এখানে কোনো মিডলম্যান (যেমন- SSLCommerz বা aamarPay) নেই। কাস্টমার পে করলে টাকা সরাসরি মার্চেন্টের নিজের bKash, Nagad, Binance বা Crypto ওয়ালেটে চলে যায়। ফলে ট্রানজেকশনের ওপর **০% ফি (Zero Platform Fees)** কাটে। \n\n### ২. এর সবচেয়ে ইউনিক ফিচারগুলো কী কী?\n* **iOS / iPhone সাপোর্ট (World First):** সাধারণত অ্যান্ড্রয়েড অ্যাপ ছাড়া পেমেন্টের SMS রিড করা যায় না। কিন্তু এরা Apple-এর ডিফল্ট **Shortcuts** অ্যাপ ব্যবহার করে একটি চমৎকার ট্রিক বের করেছে, যার ফলে আইফোন থেকেই পেমেন্টের SMS সরাসরি সার্ভারে অটোমেটিক সেন্ড (Sync) হয়ে যায়! এটি সত্যিই একটি মাস্টারপিস আইডিয়া।\n* **Fractional Offset Algorithm:** ধরুন, একই সময়ে দুজন কাস্টমার ৫০০ টাকা পে করলো। কে কোন পেমেন্ট করেছে তা বুঝবেন কীভাবে? OmniPay এই সমস্যা দূর করতে একজনকে ইনভয়েস দেয় `500.000312` টাকা এবং আরেকজনকে দেয় `500.000951` টাকার। ফলে দশমিকের পরের সংখ্যাগুলো মিলিয়ে সিস্টেম একদম ১০০% নিখুঁতভাবে পেমেন্ট কনফার্ম করতে পারে।\n* **Multi-Store (Multi-Tenant):** একটি OmniPay ইন্সটল করেই আপনি একাধিক আলাদা আলাদা মার্চেন্টকে পেমেন্ট সার্ভিস দিতে পারবেন। সবার আলাদা API Key এবং ড্যাশবোর্ড থাকবে। \n* **Dhru Fusion ও WHMCS সাপোর্ট:** এদের সিস্টেমে আগে থেকেই রেডিমেড বিলিং সফটওয়্যারের মডিউল দেওয়া আছে। \n\n### ৩. টেকনিক্যাল দিক দিয়ে কেমন?\n* এটি **Laravel 12** এবং PHP 8.2+ ব্যবহার করে বানানো।\n* এদের সিকিউরিটি অনেক হাই। ফেক পেমেন্ট ঠেকাতে Replay Attack Protection, HMAC-SHA256 সিগনেচার করা Webhook এবং লগইনে 2FA (Google Authenticator) সাপোর্ট আছে।\n* নতুন কোনো পেমেন্ট মেথড (যেমন- Stripe বা PayPal) অ্যাড করা খুবই সহজ। জাস্ট একটি PHP ক্লাস লিখে `PaymentDriverInterface` ইমপ্লিমেন্ট করলেই নতুন গেটওয়ে অ্যাড হয়ে যায়।\n\n**এককথায় বলতে গেলে:** \nএটি অত্যন্ত প্রফেশনাল এবং স্কেলেবল (Scalable) একটি প্রজেক্ট। এর README-টাও খুব সুন্দর করে লেখা, যা পড়ে যেকোনো ডেভেলপার সহজেই বুঝতে পারবে কীভাবে সিস্টেমটি কাজ করে। \n\nআপনি কি আপনার **Profess0rPay** প্রজেক্টে OmniPay-এর এই স্পেশাল ফিচারগুলো (যেমন- Fractional Offset বা iPhone Shortcut) অ্যাড করতে চাচ্ছেন, নাকি জাস্ট প্রজেক্টটি সম্পর্কে আইডিয়া নিতে চাচ্ছিলেন?","thinking":"**Prioritizing Tool Usage**\n\nI'm now focusing on tool selection, emphasizing specific tools over general ones where possible. By leveraging SMS verification, API connections, and modular gateways, you can process payments directly to your personal accounts without any middlemen.\n\n### Why Choose Profess0rPay?\n* **Zero Platform Fees:** Payments flow directly to your personal Mobile Financial Service (MFS) accounts. No intermediary taking a percentage.\n* **White-Label Branding:** Full control to change your brand name, logo, favicon, and primary colors directly from the Admin Panel.\n* **Instant Deployment:** Forget complex setups. Upload the files, hit `/install`, and the graphical wizard handles database connections and admin setup instantly.\n* **Open & Extensible:** Built on core PHP. It’s highly modular and supports continuous expansion based on community feedback.\n\n---\n\n## ✨ Core Features & Capabilities\n\n### 📱 Official Android Companion App\nManage your transactions, notifications, and gateways directly from your smartphone! Our companion app seamlessly syncs background SMS notifications to auto-verify your MFS transactions in real-time.\n**Download the official App:** [From Google Play Store](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.qubeplug.billpax_tools)\n\n### 💳 Supported Payment Methods\n- **Local MFS Gateways:** Connect bKash, Nagad, Rocket, and other Mobile Financial Services via SMS verification or direct API tokenization.\n- **Manual Gateways:** Upload custom QR codes for users to scan and pay manually.\n\n### 🛠️ Platform Capabilities\n- **2-Minute Installer**: Easy graphical setup wizard right out of the box.\n- **Payment Link Generation**: Easily create and share beautiful payment links with customers without writing any code.\n- **Developer-Ready REST API**: Connect your external eCommerce websites, apps, and billing systems effortlessly using our Secure API Keys and Scopes.\n- **Webhook Integration (IPN)**: Real-time server-to-server callbacks ensure your website instantly knows when a customer completes a payment.\n- **One-Click System Updates**: Seamlessly upgrade your Profess0rPay core with the built-in Force Re-install and Updater module.\n\n---\n\n## 🏗️ System Architecture\n\nProfess0rPay operates efficiently using core PHP and a robust MySQL database.\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n    Client[Customer Checkout] -->|Selects Method| Gateway[Profess0rPay Gateway UI]\n    Gateway --> bKash[bKash / Nagad / Rocket]\n    \n    SMS_App[Android Companion App] --> |Syncs SMS via API| ServerPool(Pending Transactions)\n    ServerPool -.-> |Matches Amount & TxID| Gateway\n    \n    Gateway --> |Status: Paid| Webhook[Webhook Dispatcher]\n    Webhook --> |Real-Time POST| MerchantSite[Merchant eCommerce Site]\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📁 Directory Structure Breakdown\n\nUnderstanding the core folders will help you confidently modify or extend the engine:\n\n```text\nProfess0rPay/\n├── assets/                     # CSS, JS, and Image assets for the UI\n├── docs/                       # Official Documentation (e.g., API_DOCUMENTATION.md)\n├── install/                    # The 2-Minute Web Setup Wizard\n├── pp-content/                 # Core System Content & Logic\n│   ├── pp-admin/               # Administrative Dashboard UI & Logic\n│   ├── pp-include/             # Core System Functions, Adapters, and Routing Logic\n│   └── pp-modules/             # Extensible Plugin System\n│       ├── pp-addons/          # System Addons\n│       ├── pp-gateways/        # Payment Gateway Drivers (bKash, Nagad, PayPal, etc.)\n│       └── pp-themes/          # Checkout UI Themes\n├── pp-media/                   # Uploaded media, SDKs, and dynamic storage\n└── index.php                   # The primary application router\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 Installation & Deployment\n\nInstalling Profess0rPay is incredibly simple.\n\n### Server Requirements\n* **PHP:** Version 8.1 or higher\n* **Database:** MySQL 5.7+ or MariaDB 10.3+\n* **PHP Extensions:** `PDO`, `pdo_mysql`, `cURL`, `mbstring`, `OpenSSL`, `JSON`\n\n### Setup Guide (cPanel / VPS)\n1. **Download:** Grab the latest release from the repository.\n2. **Upload:** Upload and extract the files to your server's public directory (e.g., `public_html` on cPanel).\n3. **Database Setup:** Create a new, empty MySQL database and a corresponding user with full privileges.\n4. **Run the Installer:** Visit your domain in a web browser (e.g., `https://yourdomain.com/`). The automatic 2-Minute Installer will greet you.\n5. **Configuration:** \n   - Enter your newly created Database Name, Username, and Password.\n   - Set up your primary Admin Account credentials.\n6. **Finish:** Once completed, the system will automatically configure your environment and log you in!\n\n---\n\n## 📚 API Documentation\n\nWant to integrate Profess0rPay into your website? Read our comprehensive developer guide!\n👉 [Read the API Documentation](docs/API_DOCUMENTATION.md)\n\n---\n\n## 🙏 Credits & Acknowledgements\n\nThis project was built to expand upon open-source payment automation capabilities. \n**Special thanks and credit** goes to the original developers of [PipraPay](https://github.com/PipraPay/PipraPay). This plugin will allow any WordPress merchant to integrate Profess0rPay instantly without writing code.\n\n## 📝 User Questions Answered\n**1. প্লাগিন বানালে আমি ওটা কোন ফোল্ডারে রাখবো?**\nআমি আপনার মেইন প্রজেক্টের রুট ডিরেক্টরিতে `downloads` বা `public/downloads` নামে একটি ফোল্ডার তৈরি করে সেখানে প্লাগিনের একটি `.zip` ফাইল (যেমন: `profess0rpay-woocommerce.zip`) রেখে দিবো। \n\n**2. ইউজার কীভাবে পাবে?**\nইউজাররা আপনার ওয়েবসাইট বা গিটহাব রিপোজিটরি থেকে এই `.zip` ফাইলটি ডাউনলোড করবে। এরপর তারা তাদের ওয়ার্ডপ্রেস ড্যাশবোর্ডে গিয়ে `Plugins -> Add New -> Upload Plugin`-এ ক্লিক করে ফাইলটি আপলোড করবে। ব্যাস, কাজ শেষ!\n\n## Proposed Plugin Architecture\nThe plugin will be built strictly following WordPress and WooCommerce developer guidelines to ensure compatibility and security.\n\n### 1. Main Plugin Structure\n- **Directory:** `profess0rpay-woocommerce/`\n- **Main File:** `profess0rpay-woocommerce.php`\n\n### 2. Plugin Class (`WC_Gateway_Profess0rPay`)\nThis class will extend `WC_Payment_Gateway` and handle the following:\n- **Settings Page:** \n  - `Enable/Disable` toggle.\n  - `Title` and `Description` (shown on checkout).\n  - `Gateway Base URL` (e.g., `https://yourdomain.com`).\n  - `Profess0rPay API Key`.\n- **Payment Processing (`process_payment`):**\n  - Extracts customer details (name, email, phone) and order total from WooCommerce.\n  - Generates the `return_url` (WooCommerce Thank You page) and `webhook_url`.\n  - Makes a secure `POST` request to `{Base URL}/api/create-payment`.\n  - Redirects the customer to the `checkout_url` provided by the API.\n- **Webhook Handling (`woocommerce_api_profess0rpay`):**\n  - Listens for the automated Webhook (IPN) sent by Profess0rPay when a payment is successful.\n  - **Security Check:** To prevent fake webhooks, it extracts the `pp_id` from the payload and calls `{Base URL}/api/verify-payment` to verify the exact status and amount directly from your server.\n  - Marks the WooCommerce order as `Processing` (Paid) and adds an order note containing the `transaction_id`.\n\n## Verification Plan\n1. I will write the complete plugin code locally inside a `scratch/profess0rpay-woocommerce` folder.\n2. I will write a script to package it into a zip file named `profess0rpay-woocommerce.zip` inside a `downloads` folder in your project root.\n3. I will backup the chat log as requested.\n4. (Manual step for you) Once completed, you can upload this zip file to any local or test WordPress site to verify it works 100% smoothly without any bugs.\n\n## User Review Required\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> Please review the architecture plan. I have included strict security checks (double verifying the webhook) so that no one can bypass the payment. 'default' => 'no'\n                )\n            );\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Process the payment and return the result.\n         */\n        public function process_payment( $order_id ) {\n            $order = wc_get_order( $order_id );\n\n            if ( empty( $this->api_key ) || empty( $this->gateway_url ) ) {\n                wc_add_notice( 'Payment Error: Gateway is not configured properly.', 'error' );\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Prepare Payload\n            $payload = array(\n                'full_name'      => $order->get_billing_first_name() . ' ' . $order->get_billing_last_name(),\n                'email_address'  => $order->get_billing_email(),\n                'mobile_number'  => $order->get_billing_phone(),\n                'amount'         => (float) $order->get_total(),\n                'currency'       => get_woocommerce_currency(),\n                'return_url'     => $this->get_return_url( $order ),\n                'webhook_url'    => add_query_arg( 'wc-api', 'profess0rpay_webhook', home_url( '/' ) ),\n                'metadata'       => json_encode( array( 'order_id' => $order_id ) )\n            );\n\n            $endpoint = $this->gateway_url . '/api/create-payment';\n            $ssl_verify = $this->get_option('disable_ssl_verify') === 'yes' ? false : true;\n\n            $args = array(\n                'method'      => 'POST',\n                'timeout'     => 30,\n                'redirection' => 5,\n                'httpversion' => '1.0',\n                'blocking'    => true,\n                'headers'     => array(\n                    'Content-Type'  => 'application/json',\n                    'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->api_key,\n                ),\n                'body'        => json_encode( $payload ),\n                'sslverify'   => $ssl_verify,\n            );\n\n            $response = wp_remote_post( $endpoint, $args );\n\n            if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) {\n                wc_add_notice( 'Connection Error: ' . $response->get_error_message(), 'error' );\n                return;\n            }\n\n            $body = wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response );\n            $data = json_decode( $body, true );\n\n            if ( isset( $data['status'] ) && $data['status'] == true && !empty( $data['checkout_url'] ) ) {\n                \n                // Remove cart\n                WC()->cart->empty_cart();\n\n                // Return redirect string\n                return array(\n                    'result'   => 'success',\n                    'redirect' => $data['checkout_url']\n                );\n            } else {\n                $error_msg = isset( $data['message'] ) ? $data['message'] : 'Unknown error from gateway.';\n                wc_add_notice( 'Gateway Error: ' . $error_msg, 'error' );\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Listen for Webhook requests from Profess0rPay.\n         */\n        public function webhook_listener() {\n            $raw_payload = file_get_contents( 'php://input' );\n            $data = json_decode( $raw_payload, true );\n\n            if ( ! $data || ! isset( $data['pp_id'] ) ) {\n                http_response_code( 400 );\n                die( 'Bad Request' );\n            }\n\n            $pp_id = sanitize_text_field( $data['pp_id'] );\n\n            // Double Verify the Payment for Security\n            $endpoint = $this->gateway_url . '/api/verify-payment';\n            $ssl_verify = $this->get_option('disable_ssl_verify') === 'yes' ? false : true;\n\n            $args = array(\n                'method'      => 'POST',\n                'timeout'     => 30,\n                'headers'     => array(\n                    'Content-Type'  => 'application/json',\n                    'Authorization' => 'Bearer ' . $this->api_key,\n                ),\n                'body'        => json_encode( array( 'pp_id' => $pp_id ) ),\n                'sslverify'   => $ssl_verify,\n            );\n\n            $response = wp_remote_post( $endpoint, $args );\n\n            if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) {\n                http_response_code( 500 );\n                die( 'Verification connection failed' );\n            }\n\n            $body = wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response );\n            $verify_data = json_decode( $body, true );\n\n            // Security Checks\n            if ( isset( $verify_data['status'] ) && $verify_data['status'] === 'completed' ) {\n                \n                $meta = $verify_data['metadata'];\n                if (is_string($meta)) {\n                    $meta = json_decode($meta, true);\n                }\n                \n                $order_id = $meta['order_id'] ?? 0;\n                $order = wc_get_order( $order_id );\n\n                if ( ! $order ) {\n                    http_response_code( 404 );\n                    die( 'Order not found' );\n                }\n\n                // Duplicate payment protection\n                if ( $order->is_paid() || $order->has_status( 'completed' ) || $order->has_status( 'processing' ) ) {\n                    http_response_code( 200 );\n                    die( 'Order already processed' );\n                }\n\n                // Amount Verification\n                $api_amount = (float) $verify_data['amount'];\n                $order_amount = (float) $order->get_total();\n\n                if ( abs($api_amount - $order_amount) > 0.01 ) {\n                    $order->update_status( 'on-hold', 'Payment received but amount mismatch. Expected: ' . $order_amount . ' Received: ' . $api_amount );\n                    http_response_code( 200 );\n                    die( 'Amount mismatch recorded' );\n                }\n\n                // Payment Success!\n                $transaction_id = isset( $verify_data['transaction_id'] ) ? $verify_data['transaction_id'] : '';\n                $gateway_name   = isset( $verify_data['gateway'] ) ? $verify_data['gateway'] : 'Profess0rPay';\n                \n                $order->payment_complete( $transaction_id );\n                $order->add_order_note( \"Payment completed via $gateway_name. TrxID: $transaction_id\" );\n                \n                http_response_code( 200 );\n                die( 'Webhook Processed Successfully' );\n            }\n\n            http_response_code( 400 );\n            die( 'Payment not verified or not completed' );\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Register Gateway\nadd_filter( 'woocommerce_payment_gateways', 'profess0rpay_add_gateway_class' );\nfunction profess0rpay_add_gateway_class( $gateways ) {\n    $gateways[] = 'WC_Gateway_Profess0rPay';\n    return $gateways;\n}\n","Description":"Create main WooCommerce plugin file with security implementations.","Overwrite":true,"TargetFile":"c:\\xampp\\htdocs\\Profess0rPay\\scratch\\profess0rpay-woocommerce\\profess0rpay-woocommerce.php","toolAction":"Write plugin code","toolSummary":"Write profess0rpay-woocommerce.php"}}]}
